NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
CARBON INDUSTRIES (PRIVATE) LTD
611 OLD NO. 186/187, T.H. ROAD, CHENNAI-600 081.
“Carbon Industries Private Limited having its registered Office at 611 Old No. 186/187, Thiruvottiyur High Road,
Chennai-600 081, in its Extraordinary General Meeting held on 14-11-2012 at 10.30 AM at registered Office had passed
a resolution for winding up the Company Voluntarily.”
Chennai,
28th November 2012.

Megharaj N. Kathare
Director.
(Rajaram N. Kathare)
Director.

3056

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

CARBON INDUSTRIES (PRIVATE) LIMITED
611, Old No. 186/187, T.H. Road, Chennai-600 081
Copy of resolution passed in the Extra-ordinary General meeting of the shareholders of Carbon Industries Private
Limited on Wednesday the 14th November 2012 at 10.30 AM at the registered office of the company at
611 Old No. 186/187, Thiruvottiyur High Road, Chennai-600 081.
To pass the special resolution for the winding up of the company, the Chairman explained that it would not be
profitable or benefit for the Company to resume its activities in view of the high cost involved. The other members agreed
with the Chairman.
The following resolution was proposed by Sri. Maruthi, R. Kathare and seconded by Sri. Kiran M. Kathare.
“Resolved that the company be wound up voluntarily under Section 484 of the Companies Act.” Carried Unanimously.

Chennai,
28th November 2012

Megharaj N. Kathare
Director.
Rajaram N. Kathare
Director.

FORM No. 155
(See rule 329)
Member Voluntary Winding up
QUICK THREAD PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd. Office 214, Velacherry Tambaram Main Road, Pallikkaranai, Chennai-600 100.
Notice Convening Final Meeting of Contributions.
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a general meeting of the members of the above named
company will be held at Door No. 214, Velacherry-Tambaram Main Road, Pallikkaranai, Chennai-600 100, Tamil Nadu
on the 29th day of December 2012 at 11.30 a.m. for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing the
manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the Company disposed of and hearing any
explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also determining by a special resolution of the Company, the manner
in which the books, account , and documents of the Company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
29th November 2012.

KENNETH VICTOR ABRAHAM,
(Liquidator.)
